* Har musibat, bala ane aafat si hifazat thay che.
* Dushman na shar si pan bachav thay che.
* Gham, pareshaani ane tension door thay che.
* Rizq ma barkat ane rozi ma was'at aave che.
* Dil ne sukoon ane chain hasil thay che.
* Bimari si shifa ane sehat naseeb thay che.
* Gunaah ni maghfirat ane rehmat naseeb thay che.

*_رات ما اُتهي نے پهلے نماز نو پرھنار وضوء كرے_*
 
*_وضوء ني نية 'ا مثل لے_*

*_Raat Ma Uthi Ne Pehle Namaz No Parhnar Wuzu Kare , Wuzu Ni Niyyat Aa 2 Ma Si Koi Bhi Leso To Chalse , Niyyat Aa Misal Le._*

*`1) اَللّهُمَّ اِنِّيْ نَوَيْتُ اَنْ اَتَوَضَّأُ لِصَلوةِ الَّيْلِ وَالتَّهَجُّدِ وَلِكُلِّ صَلوةٍ اُصَلِّيْهَا`*

*`2) اَّللّهُمَّ اِنِّيْ نَوَيْتُ طَهُوْرِيْ 'هذَا لِصَلوةِ النِّصْفِ الَّيْلِ وَلِكُلِّ صَلوةٍ اُصَلِّيْهَا`*

*_رات ما نماز پرهوا نے اُتهے انے نصف االيل نا وقت نے دير هوئي تو تحميد و صلوات ني بيجي نمازو جه چاهے تے پرھے._*

*_Raat Ma Namaz Parhwa Ne Uthe Anne Nisfil Lail Na Waqat Ne Dair Hoi To Tahmid Wa Salawaat Ni Biji Namazo Je Chahe Te Parhe._*

*_انے نصف االيل نو وقت تهائي تو پهلے استفتاح ني ٢ ركعة نماز پرهي نے  نصف اليل ني ٢ ركعة نماز پرهے  انے تے بعد بیجی نمازو پرهے . شفع وتر انے جلوس ني نماز رات ني سگلي نمازو نا پچھي پرهے.._*

*_Anne Nisfil Lail No Waqat Thai To Pehle Istiftah Ni 2 Rakat Namaz Parhi Ne Nisfil Lail Ni 2 Rakat Namaz Parhe.  Anne Te Baad Biji Namazo Parhe.  Shafe'a,  Watar Anne Julus Ni Namaz Raat Ni Sagli Namazo Na Pachi Parhe._*
 
*_شفع ني نماز پرها پجهي فجر ني نماز نو وقت تهائے تے پھلا کوئي نماز پرهے تو شفع ني نماز والوي پرهے ._*

*_Shaf'a Ni Namaz Parha Pachi Fajar Ni Namaz No Waqat Thai Te Pehla Koi Namaz Parhe To Shaf'a Ni Namaz Walwi Parhe._*

2/20/26, 4:23 AM - +91 98756 84551: **Religious Fasting/Ramadan**
**Fasting Advice for Diabetics**

Religious Ramadan Fasting entails refraining from eating and drinking water/liquids from sunrise to sunset, and it generally leads to the consumption of larger meals at night.
This can affect blood glucose levels adversely!

Due to having evolved as day active beings, our innate clock and delicate endocrine function behaves accordingly: it performs best in-between sunrise and sunset.

Therefore blood glucose levels are considerably better balanced by consuming food during the day, whilst being active.
A Ramadan Diabetes Diet should be simple and basic.

During Ramadan the early morning Sahar meal is unlikely to contribute to poorly balanced blood glucose levels, especially if whole grain preparations are consumed in combination with high fibre vegetables and moderate, sensible servings of protein.

Food intake after sunset requires balance and some restraint.
It is best to keep a close check on blood glucose levels during Ramadan (glucometer self-monitoring) in order to be aware of blood glucose fluctuations.

Remember that frequent blood glucose spikes do have a negative effect on overall health.

Health Tips for Diabetics during Ramadan:
Don’t s: 
• Sugary drinks, ‘soft’ drinks, fruit juices, liquidized fruits [sweetened, unsweetened, even home-made]
• Highly processed foods
• Junk foods
• Oily, fatty foods, ‘rich’, processed foods at night [Iftar]
• Bananas, very sweet fruits
• Excessive intake of fruits, dried fruits
• Overeating
• Sedentary lifestyle
Do s
• Increase the consumption of high fibre vegetables, green leafy vegetables
• Eat plenty of vegetable salads, whilst avoiding/minimizing mayonnaise, salad cream. Use traditional salad dressing
• Include more fresh foods
• Consume fibre rich starch/complex carbohydrates at Sahar (meal before sunrise), i.e. red rice, upuma, rotti prepared with whole grain varieties of flour, combined with above
• Increase water intake at permitted times
• Moderate fruit consumption (semi-sweet only!)
• Eat slowly and chew well to aid digestion and prevent overeating
• Reduce salt/sodium intake to minimize thirst, to maintain well balanced blood pressure and to preserve kidney function
• Maintain moderate activity levels
• Drink only water and moderate quantities of tea, herbal tea, green tea/coffee without sugar.

If diabetic control is poor prior Fasting, further damage to overall health is possible due to changes of meal timing, wake/sleep pattern and decreased levels of activity.

Please consult your healthcare specialist if/how your blood glucose can be managed satisfactorily during Ramadan Fasting to be able to maintain best possible Diabetes Wellness.

5/12/25, 2:42 PM - +92 310 0674553: I agree. 
While it's a straightforward way to get responses, it can sometimes lead to a lot of notifications and make it harder to keep track of other important messages.

I was thinking that for requests like these, it might be helpful to use a shared Excel sheet instead. People could easily add their names there, and it would keep the main chat clearer for general communication. It might also look a bit more organized.

Just a humble suggestion! What do you all think? 😊

5/13/25, 5:28 PM - Ammar Sehorewala: Salaam bhaiyo, 

Je sagla ne Hizb mili gaya che and ehna hizb na logo ni request che regarding 'Hizb Internal Change' to ehma aa 3 cheezo hase toj group change ni request consider karva ma aavse : 

- *Mard ane ehna bairo alag thai gaya hoi* 
- *Farzand ane ehna ma bawa alag thai gaya hoi* 
- *Caretaker and dependent or beneficiary alag thai gaya hoi*
- Request ch ke jem format message niche aapu ch ehma barabr si personal par mne message kare
- Talabat (Masool) na if azwaaj alag thai gaya hoi bija ahzaab  ma to bhi likewise msg kare
5/13/25, 5:28 PM - Ammar Sehorewala: *Format of Message* 

Je particular mumin na group change ni request aavi che ehni aa misal details bhare...
 
 _Name_ - 
 _ITS_ - 
 _Haj ID_ -
 _His/ Her *Hizb No*_ - 
 _Want to change to *Hizb No*_ - 
 _Reason_ -

1/4/26, 11:28 AM - Mufaddal Kothari: @⁨Meta AI⁩ are all mushrooms halal?
1/4/26, 11:28 AM - Meta AI: Most mushrooms are halal, meaning permissible under Islamic law, as long as they're not poisonous or harmful to health. Since mushrooms are plant-based and grow naturally, they're generally considered halal. However, you need to be cautious about poisonous types like death cap or fly agaric, as consuming them is haram (forbidden) due to health risks.

The key principle is: if a mushroom is safe and beneficial, it's halal. So, stick to edible varieties like button or oyster mushrooms, and avoid wild ones unless you're sure they're safe ¹ ² ³.

1/11/26, 7:59 PM - Meta AI: You meant "sarees," right? 😊 Sarees have been around for over 5,000 years, dating back to the Indus Valley Civilization (2600-1900 BCE). They're mentioned in ancient texts like the Rig Veda (3000 B.C.) and depicted in sculptures from the 1st to 6th centuries. The word "sari" means "strip of cloth" in Sanskrit, evolving from three-piece ensembles like antariya (lower garment), uttariya (veil), and stanapatta (chestband) ¹ ² ³.

Want to know more about saree draping styles or their cultural significance? Want to explore iconic saree types like Banarasi or Kanchipuram? 🧵

* Sagla Mumineen Mumenaat farzando aa mehmaan ni karamat kare, ibadat ma mashgool rahe, 1 na khuda 70 aape che, barabar ganimat lai, 5 faraz imamat si parhe, adeyat shareefah tilawat, bihori ni namaz, tasbeehul aazam ni namaz, *muwasaat* na amalo, iftar karawanu che, ehma bhi ijtehaad kare
* Quran ni tilawat zyada si zyada mumeneen kare ehna waaste Burhanuddin Moula RA irshadaat farmawta, ye j misal Syedna Mufaddal Saifuddin Aqa TUS irshadat farmawi rhya che
* Mumineen har roz Quran ni tilawat kare ane shehrullah ma ghani zyada kare
* 1 din ma ghana mumineen ehwa hoi che je pura quran khatam kare che ehni tehseen farmawi
* *3 Quran* to khatam kare j sagla mumeneen, mumenaat ane farzando em Moula TUS ni ummeed che
* Aa silat ane muwasaat na mahina che, khabargiri kare madad kare
* Sagla khidmatguzaro mumeneen ek bija ne silat kare, muwasaat kare, kaam aawe, takleef dur karwani koshish kare.
* Aqa Moula TUS ye farmayu Dubai ma ke Tamam mumineen khidmatguzaro darwaza par dastak dai, darwaza thoki ne, ne aagal si rai ne silat kare, madad kare.
* Quran ni tilawat (3 Quran khatam) ane Muwasat ane Silat (Aagal si rai ne khidmat karwu madad karwu) - Aa 2 amal na waaste khaas irshadaat aaliyah farmaya che.
* Ek mumin ye 21 karbala ni ticket ni khidmat karse em araz kidi - Moula tus ye farmayu ke aa silat ane muwasaat nu bhi amal karso? Kai tarah karso?
* Moze par communication shuru kari de aa 2 amal waaste khaas.
* Hygiene nu khaas khayal rakhwu jaman ma, quality barabar hoi, ek kharas ek meethaas na nizam mutabiq
* Rooh na mehel ma Husain Imam AS ni zikar, 1 aansu na badal 8 jannat - *Jannat kharidta jaajo kharidta jajo kharidta jajo* em farmayu

2/10/26, 3:00 PM - Meta AI: Sila Fitra ki raqam ka elaan ho chuka hai, jo ki Rs. 220 per person hai, jo wheat ke hesab se hai. Agar aap dates, raisins, ya dried apricots ke hesab se Sila Fitra ada karna chahte hain, to raqam kuch yun hai:
- Dates: Rs. 1,650 per person
- Raisins: Rs. 2,500 per person
- Dried Apricots: Rs. 5,000 per person

Yeh raqam Pakistan ke liye hai, aur aapke ilaqe ke muqami shura ke mutabiq Sila Fitra ki raqam fark ho sakti hai. Aap apne ilaqe ke muqami shura se maloomat kar sakte hain ¹ ² ³.

Aap Sila Fitra ki raqam ka elaan Eid-ul-Fitr se pehle ada kar sakte hain, taaki needmand liyon ko Eid-ul-Fitr manane ka mauqa mil sake.

2/19/26, 1:13 PM - Mufaddal Kothari: @⁨Meta AI⁩ what if I have not memorized Surah al Shams and Surah al Gashiyah for the prayer of Nisf ul Lail ? Which surah can I pray instead?
2/19/26, 1:13 PM - Meta AI: If you haven't memorized Surah Al-Shams and Surah Al-Gashiyah, you can recite other Surahs in the prayer of Nisf ul-Lail (Tahajjud prayer or any other voluntary night prayer).

You can recite any Surah or verses from the Quran that you've memorized. Some common alternatives include:
- Surah Al-Fatiha followed by shorter Surahs like Surah Al-Ikhlas, Surah Al-Falaq, or Surah Al-Nas.
- Other Surahs like Surah Al-Baqarah (verses 1-5 or other parts), Surah Al-Kafirun, or Surah Al-Mulk.

It's best to consult a scholar or imam for specific guidance on prayers and recitations.

Would you like more info on Nisf ul-Lail prayer or alternative Surahs?

You can recite:
- Surah Al-Fatiha followed by shorter Surahs like Surah Al-Ikhlas, Surah Al-Falaq, or Surah Al-Nas.
- Other Surahs like Surah Al-Kafirun, Surah Al-Mulk, or Surah Al-Muzzammil.

Choose Surahs that are easy for you to recite and allow for a meaningful prayer experience for the congregation.
